SKYE BA NGO BO NYID MED PA DANG, YONGS

SU GRUB PA LA DON DAM PA NGO BO NYID MED PA'I PHYIR RO, ,MA
SKYES PA MA 'GAGS PA GZOD MA NAS ZHI BA RANG BZHIN GYIS MYA NGAN
LAS 'DAS PA ZHES 'BYUNG BA'I DGONGS PA

GANG YIN ZHE NA, JI LTAR NGO BO NYID MED PA DE LTAR MA SKYES SO,
,JI LTAR MA SKYES PA DE LTAR MA 'GAGS SO, ,JI LTAR MA SKYES PA
DANG MA 'GAGS PA DE LTAR GZOD MA NAS

@037B ZHI BA'O, ,DE LTAR RANG BZHIN GYIS YONGS SU MYA NGAN LAS
'DAS SO, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA BZHIN NGO BO NYID MED TSUL MTSAN NYID
GSUM GA'I DBANG DU BYAS NAS GSUNGS

TSUL 'DI YANG GONG GI MDO SDE DGONGS 'GREL DANG SUM CU PA RNAMS
KYIS GSUNGS PA DANG MTHUN PAS ZUR DU 'GREL MI DGOS SO, ,DES NA,
'GREL CHEN LAS NI SKYE

MED 'GAGS MED GNYIS KYI DGONGS GZHIR GZHAN DBANG MI 'JOG PA YANG
RTEN CING 'BREL PAR 'BYUNG BA'I DON MED PA MIN PAR BSTAN PA'I
PHYIR YIN LA, ZHES

MDO'I DGONGS PA LEN PAR MDZAD CING, KUN LAS BTUS LAS NI GZHAN
DBANG BDAG NYID LAS SKYE BA MED PA DANG RGYU MED LAS SKYE BA MED
PA'I DBANG DU BYAS NAS BSHAD PAS,

'GAL BA MED DO, ,YANG GZHAN DBANG DE GZOD MA NAS ZHI BA DANG,
RANG BZHIN GYIS YONGS SU MYA NGAN LAS 'DAS PA GNYIS KYI DGONGS
GZHIR MI 'JOG PA YANG KUN NAS

NYON MONGS KYIS BSDUS PA SHAS CHE BAS MA BZHAG LA, NGO BO NYID
MED TSUL GSUM GYI SKABS SU MTSAN NYID GSUM GA LA DGONGS TSUL
YANG LEGS BSHAD SNYING POR

@038A *, ,NGO BO NYID GSUM GYI RANG RANG GI SKABS KYI NGO BO MED
RGYU DE'I DBANG DU BYAS NAS JI LTAR NGO BO NYID MED PA DE LTAR
MA SKYES PA DANG MA 'GAGS LA GZOD MA

'DI'I DGONGS GZHI

LEN LUGS LA YANG TSIG ZIN LA MI 'DRA BA CUNG ZAD RE 'DUG KYANG

PAR BYA'O, ,GSUM PA, NGO BO

NYID GSUM GYI NGO BO NGOS BZUNG BA LA KUN BTAGS NGOS BZUNG BA
NI, DGONGS 'GREL LAS, RNAM PAR RTOG PA'I SPYOD YUL KUN BTAGS
PA'I MTSAN NYID

KYI GNAS 'DU BYED KYI MTSAN MA LA GZUGS KYI PHUNG PO ZHES NGO BO

NYID DU MING DANG BRDAS RNAM PAR

@038B BZHAG PA GANG LAGS PA DE NI KUN BTAGS PA'I MTSAN NYID LAGS
TE, ZHES GSUNGS, DE'I DON NI, RNAM PAR RTOG PA'I SPYOD YUL ZHES
PA'I SKABS SU RNAM PAR RTOG

PA NI KUN BTAGS 'DOGS BYED KYI RTOG PA YIN LA, DE'I SPYOD YUL NI
DE'I ZHEN YUL GZHAN DBANG DANG, GZHAN DBANG DE LA KUN BTAGS PA'I
TSUL NI 'DI NI GZHAN

DBANG NGO, 'DI NI GZHAN DBANG GI SKYE BA'O ZHES NGO BO DANG
KHYAD PAR GYI SGO NAS 'DOGS SHING, DE LTAR 'DOGS PA'I GNAS SU
GZHAN DBANG NYID 'JOG PAS GNAS ZHES

SBYAR LA, GZHAN DBANG DE LA GZHAN DBANG ZHES PA'I MING DANG
GZHAN DBANG GI SKYE BA ZHES PA'I KHYAD PAR GYI TSIG LA BLTOS NAS
'DU BYED KYI MTSAN MA 'JOG DGOS

PAS NA 'DU BYED KYI MTSAN MA ZHES SBYAR RO, ,DE YANG GDAGS GZHI
GZHAN DBANG, DE NYID KUN BTAGS 'DOGS PA'I GZHIR 'GRO TSUL GSUM
GYI SGO NAS BTAGS

'DZIN TSUL YANG

@056B TSUL YANG GZHAN DBANG GI DNGOS PO RNAMS NI KHO RANG GI NGO
BO SHES PA LA GTUG DGOS SHING, KHO RANG DANG NGO BO GCIG PA'I
SHES PA DE NYID DE NYAMS

SU MYONG BA'I RANG RIG GIS 'JOG PA YIN LA, DE'I RGYU MTSAN GYIS
RANG MTSAN BRJOD MED KYI BRJOD DU MED PA DANG, DON DAM PA YOD PA
DANG YANG

DAG PAR YOD PA RNAMS KYI DON RANG RIG GI NGOR YOD TSUL DANG
SBYOR DGOS PAS, DON DU NA GZHAN DBANG GI DNGOS PO THAMS CAD KYI
GRUB TSUL

JI LTA BA BZHIN RANG RIG LA SNANG BA LTAR YIN PAS, DE LTAR SNANG
BA LTAR GRUB PA'I DON DE NYID RANG GI MTSAN NYID KYIS GRUB, PA'I
CHA THAMS CAD

KYI SGO NAS RNAM PA THAMS CAD DU MED DO, ZHES SKUR PA 'DEBS PA
DES NI DNGOS PO'I YOD TSUL DANG YIN TSUL JI LTA BA BZHIN LAS
NYAMS TE CHUD

ZOS PAR BYAS PA YIN LA, SGRO SKUR GNYIS KYIS DNGOS PO'I GNAS
TSONG LAS NYAMS PAR BYAS PA GANG YIN PA 'DIS NI, LTA BA GTAN LA
PHAB TE

BYAS

BRTEN PA'I CHAGS

MTHONG NAS STER

PAR BDAG DANG SLOB MA'I TSOGS RNAMS KYANG, ,TSUL 'DI BSHAD SGRUB
GNYIS

KYIS 'DZIN PA NA, ,'GAL RKYEN KUN ZHI MTHUN RKYEN KUN TSANG NAS,
,SPYAN RAS GZIGS DBANG NYID DANG MTSUNGS PAR SHOG, CES BSTAN
BCOS

LEGS PAR BSHAD PA'I SNYING PO'I 'GREL PA 'DI YANG SNGON NAS,
GANGS CAN BSTAN 'GRO YONGS KYI LHA GCIG THAMS CAD MKHYEN GZIGS

@390A *, ,CHEN PO'I DRUNG NAS RGYAS LA DPYIS PHYIN PA ZHIG STZAL
DGOS ZHES YANG YANG NAN GYIS SNYAN SGRON GSOL BAR ZHAL GYIS

BZHES SHING, DE NAS ZHAL BSKUL YANG YANG ZHUS KYANG YONG GSUNG
BA LAS DNGOS SU 2 BKA' RTZOM GNANG THUB PA ZHIG MA BYUNG BAR LUS

PA DANG, DE'I BAR SKABS SHIG TU DGE SLONG DGE 'DUN 'GYUR MED
LAGS NAS KYANG DVOGS GNAS RNAMS LA DMIGS PHUG GIS 'DI DANG

'DI ZHIB RGYAS PHEBS DGOS TSUL GYI ZHABS BSKUL SHOG BSGRIL DANG
BCAS PA GSOL DPON GRAGS PA MTHA' YAS LAGS BRGYUD NAS

GSOL BA BTAB PAR, DGYES PA CHEN POS ZHAL GYIS BZHES PAR MDZAD PA
DANG, DE NAS BZUNG DGE SLONG 'GYUR MED LAGS LA YANG MJAL

KHAR PHEBS RES BZHIN THUGS DAM 'PHEL PO AE BYUNG GSUNG BA'I BKA'
'DRI DNGOS SU PHEBS NAS RJES 'DZIN GZHAN DANG MI 'DRA BA GNANG
ZHING,

@390B DE LTAR GNANG BA'I RTEN 'BREL GYI DBANG GIS DRA LAN 'DIR
YANG DGE SLONG 'GYUR, MED LAGS NAS BSKUL BA PO MDZAD PA DANG,
SPYIR YANG, DE

NAS 'DI PHYI'I LEGS PHYOGS JI SNYED PA, RTEN 'BREL LEGS PAR
'GRIG PA'I RTZA BA NI, LAM STON BSHES GNYEN DAM PA ZHES GSUNGS
PA LTAR YIN

PAS NA, BDAG GIS KYANG BSTAN BCOS LEGS PAR BSHAD PA'I SNYING
PO'I 'GREL PA 'DI LTA BU RTZOM PA'I SKAL PA THOB PA NI, 7BLA MA
DAM PA DUS

GSUM SANGS RGYAS THAMS CAD LAS KYANG BKA' DRIN LHAG PA DE LTA
BUS DGYES BZHIN DU 'DI'I 'GREL PA MDZAD PAR ZHAL GYIS BZHES PA'I
RTEN 'BRAL

GYI MTHU KHO NAR GO ZHING, DE YANG, RANG GI NGOS NAS KYANG TSIG
BSGRIL GYIS BSTAN BCOS 'DI'I DON LA BSHAD LUNG KHRID SOGS DANG,
DMIGS RNAMS

KYANG RGYUN CHAGS SU YID LA BYAS TE, DKA' GNAD RNAMS LA MTHA'
BCAD KHUL GYI DGA' BA DANG SPOBS PA RGYUN CHAGS SU YOD NA'ANG,
DA LAN

@391A *, ,'DI RTZOM SKABS SNGAR GYI DE LAS KYANG HA CANG MI
'DRA BAR SHES RAB GSAL SHING MYUR BA DANG, DKA' GNAD RNAMS
KYANG

RANG BABS KYIS 'GREL NUS PA BYUNG ZHING, DE LTAR BYUNG BA'I
SKABS RNAMS SU 'DI LTA BU BYUNG BA DE NYID GANG GI MTHUS YIN
SNYAM DU YA

MTSAN CHEN PO SKYES NAS, RANG LA YANG YID MI CHES PA'I TSOD LTA
BU BYUNG BA NA, DE LA ZHIB TU BSAMS PAS DE NI SNGAR, 7 GONG SA
SKYABS

MGON MCHOG LA BSTAN BCOS 'DI'I 'GREL PA ZHIB CING RGYAS LA DBYIS
PHYIN BA ZHIS DGOS ZHES YANG YANG NAN GYIS GSOL BAR DGYES BZHIN

DU YONG GSUNG BA'I RTEN 'BREL DANG, DE LTAR YONG GSUNG BA LAS
BKA' RTZOM DNGOS SU MA GNANG BAR DA BAR LUS PA 'DI LA DA RES DGE

SLONG 'GYUR MED LAGS NAS BSKUL MA GTZO BOR MDZAD PA DANG, RANG
GIS KYANG DANG DU BLANGS NAS RTZOM PA 'DI LA SNGAR GYI RTEN
'BREL DE

@391B THAMS CAD 'DZOM PA'I MTHUS, 7 GONG SA MCHOG GI BYIN RLABS
DNGOS SU ZHUGS PA RANG LOS YIN SNYAM PA'I MOS GUS LHAG PAR CHE
BA

BYUNG BAS NA, 'GREL PA 'DI NYID RTZOM PA PO KHO BO YIN KYANG,
BYIN RLABS KYI, RGYU NI 7 GONG SA MCHOG GI YIN PAR THAG NGES

PAR CHOD PA DE BZHIN YIN PAS, GROGS MCHOG BLO LDAN RNAMS LA NANG
LUGS, SNYING GTAM KHO NAR ZHUS PA 'DI LA

THUGS YID CHES PAR MDZAD NAS, BSTAN BCOS 'DI'I DON LA ZHUGS TE
THOS DON SGRUB PA SNYING POR BYA BA RIGS SO,, ,,

3 DE YANG BSTAN BCOS LEGS PAR BSHAD PA'I SNYING PO 'DI'I DON LA
RGYUN DU 'DRIS PA DANG DO GAL CHE, ZHING THOS DON SGRUB PA LA

GZHOL BA BSGRUB DON SNYING POR, 'DRIL BA, BSHES GNYEN CHEN PO,
DGE SLONG 'GYUR MED LAGS KYI GTZO BOR MDZAD,

@392A *, ,BSHES GNYEN DAM PA RAB 'BYAMS PA NGAG DBANG RGYA MTSO
DANG, BKRA SHIS DGON GSAR BA'I GNAS DGE SLONG BLO BZANG RIN CHEN
DANG, DAG SLONG BLO GROS DPAL 'BAR, BSHAD

SGRUB GNYIS KYI SGO NAS 'DZIN SKYONG SBEL GSUM NUS PA'I DGE BA'I
BSHES GNYEN CHEN PO DKA' CHEN BLO BZANG DKON MCHOG GIS, BSKUL BA
PO DANG YI GE'I CHA RKYEN GNYIS GA MDZAD CING,

BSAM YAS RAB BYUNG BA'I GNAS BLA MA'I CHAR GTOGS DGE SLONG BLO
BZANG DGE LEGS SOGS THAMS CAD NAS MGRIN GCIG GIS BSKUL BA'I
NGOR, BLA MA DAM PA RNAMS KYIS

RJES SU BZUNG ZHING, SH'AKYA'I BSTAN LA DGE SLONG GI DNGOS PO
THOB PA TSE DANG SGRUB PA MNYAM PA'I SER BYAS RAB 'BYAMS SMRA BA
BLO BZANG DGE LEGS KYIS DBEN PA'I GNAS MCHOG

BA BAL GYI RKED TSANG RI KHROD DU SBYAR BA'O, , ` SVA STE, AE MA
LEGS BSHAD SNYING PO'I DKA' 'GREL 'DI, BSTAN PA 'DZIN SKYONG
SKYES BU DAM PA DANG, SKAL LDAN BLO GSAL

RNAMS LA PHAN PHYIR DU, DBUS SMAD ZAL MO SGANG GI SA YI CHA,
RDZA RGYUD BKRA SHIS BSAM 'GRUB DGON CHEN GYI, BLA BRANG YA ZUR
RGYAL MTSAN MTHON PO NAS, ,

@392B RVA LO SPRUL MING BLO BZANG DPAL LDAN PA, RNAM RGYAL GRUB
PA'I RDO RJE BDAG GIS GTZOS, NGAG DBANG BLO BZANG BYAMS PA BSTAN
'PHAL DANG, MDZOD PA BLO BZANG DPAL LDAN LA SOGS

PA, BDAG CAG LTOS PAR BCAS PA THAMS CAD KYIS, NGAL BA CHEN PO'I
PAR 'DI BSKRUN PA'I DGES, BDE SKYID NYI SHAR RGYAL KHAMS BDE
RGYUR CIG STON PA'I GSUNG RAB RIN CHEN GLEGS BAM

GYIS, 'GRO BA YONGS LA PHAN THOG 'BYUNG BA LTAR, BDAG CAG RNAMS
KYIS GLEGS BAM 'DI BZHENGS PA'I, MTHONG THOS 'GRO LA PHAN THOG
RGYA CHEN SHOG LI GE GCIG LAS BRGYA STONG KHRI

'BUM SOGS, DKA' CHOG MAD PAR MANG POR 'PHEL BYED PA, DPE 'DI
GANG GI PAR SHING 'DON PA DANG, NYAMS SU LEN CING SAN RE THOS
PAS KYANG, MI DGE SDIG PA'I BSAM SBYOR

SHUGS KYI 'GAGS, RNAM DKAR DGE BA DANG GI 'PHEL BAR SHOG GLEGS
BAM GANG DU BZHUGS PA'I SA PHYOGS SU, NAD MUG 'KHRUG RTZOD MING
YANG MI GRAGS SHING, LO LEGS NOR

KUN 'KHYIL BAR SHOG CES DRANG BA DANG NGES PA'I DON RNAM PAR
'BYED PA'I BSTAN BCOS LEGS BSHAD PA'I SNYING PO'I DGONGS DON
GSAL

@393A *, ,BAR BYED PA'I ME SONG ZHES BYA BA 'DI NYID RGYAS BSDUS
'CHAM ZHING, RANG RE'I YIG CHA DANG KHOG GCIG PAR SNANG BA DANG,
GZHUNG SPYI'I

RIG SAM 'TSOL BA LA LEGS BSHAD RMAD DU BYUNG BAR BRTEN, BLO GSAL
DON GNYER CAN RNAMS LA PHAN BA RGYA CHER 'BYUNG BA DANG, RANG
GZHAN KUN GYI

BDE LEGS KYI 'BYUNG GNAS SU NGES PA'I LHAG BSAM RNAM DAG GYI SGO
NAS, DBU MDZAD MGON PO BSAM GRUB NAS PAR GSAR BSKRUN THOG SHING
YOS LO

RVA LO AER TE NE MER GAN HO THOG THU BLO BZANG DPAL LDAN RNAM
RGYAL GRUB PA'I RDO RJES, MKHAS MANG BYE BA'I 'BYUNG GNAS SER
BYES GVRA TSANG GI CHOS GRVAR LHA LDAN

SMON LAM CHEN MO'I GRA SKOR MING BTAGS KYI SNGON 'GRE'I DAM BCA'
'JOG SKABS RTEN 'BYUNG LEGS CHA DANG 'BRAS BAR SBYOR 'JAG BGYIS
PA'I PAR BYANG SMON
